Crisp gold\n# (Doc.label) is preserved by build_record. ~1345 clean rows available.\n#\n# Reused primitives (signatures verified in SRC):\n#   st.knockoff_plus_threshold(W, alpha)->(T,n_adm_pos,ratio)  [ratio == decoy_fdr_hat]\n#   st.W_signed_max(zr,zd);  st._knockoff_fast / _realized_fast (vectorized, bootstrap hot loop)\n#   st.tail_win_rate(list[(zr,zd)], cut)->(winrate,n_tail)  [decoy wins iff zd>zr]\n#   st.doc_block_bootstrap(doc_arrays, stat_fn, B, seed)->{ci_low,ci_high}\n#   st.rank_normalize(pool_dict, seed);  st.k_floor(alpha) -> {0.05:20,0.1:10,0.2:5,0.3:4,0.5:2}\n#   st.ks_two_sample / mannwhitney / anderson_darling_2samp / permutation_two_sample\n#   st.benjamini_hochberg(pvals,q);  fc.plain_threshold_gate(Z,alpha)\n#   llm_client.OpenRouterClient.call(model, messages, max_tokens, temperature, seed, sample_idx)\n#   method.extract_doc / gen_counterfactual_decoys / gen_swaps / score_portable / analyze_crux\n#   method.diagonal_for_family / _pairs_for / _decoy_map / norm_pool  (the diagonal + paired block)\n\nCONSTANTS:\n  ALPHA_GRID = [0.05,0.10,0.20,0.30,0.50]; TAU=0.05; N_FALSE_MIN=40; K_SC=5; B_BOOT=2000\n  DENSITIES   = [0.20, 0.50, 0.85]            # target genuine-FALSE fraction of scored real pool\n  ACC_THRESHOLD = 0.45                         # Phase-0 competent-extractor bar (>> 0.17)\n  SOFT_CAP_USD = 4.0; HARD_STOP_USD = 10.0\n  EXTRACTOR_CANDIDATES = ['openai/gpt-4.1-mini','openai/gpt-4o-mini','openai/gpt-4.1']  # probe order cheap->dear\n  FAMILIES = ['multi_hop','atomic']            # multi_hop is the registered populable family; atomic for contrast\n\n############################################################################\n# STAGE 0 -- OFFLINE SELFTEST (no API). Extend SRC/method.selftest().\n############################################################################\n# Keep ALL existing asserts. ADD:\n#  (1) subsample_to_density(): on a synthetic pool of labelled reals it returns a\n#      subset whose realized FALSE fraction == target within +/-1/pool_size, and\n#      every returned cand keeps its doc_id (doc blocks intact).\n#  (2) persistence-cell logic on two synthetic fixtures: (a) PAIRED-FAILS fixture\n#      (false reals' zr deterministically > their decoy zd) => paired win-rate CI_high<0.5\n#      AND realized FDR > alpha with CI_low>alpha; (b) PAIRED-OK fixture (fair coin)\n#      => win-rate CI covers 0.5 AND realized FDR <= alpha. Assert the EARNED/SCOPED\n#      classifier returns the right label on each.\n# Run: uv run method.py --selftest  (must pass before any API call).\n\n############################################################################\n# STAGE 1 -- PHASE-0 EXTRACTOR PROBE (pick the competent extractor)  [~$0.1-0.3]\n############################################################################\ndef phase0_probe(candidates, pilot_docs ~ 40 docs):\n  for model in candidates:\n     run method.extract_doc(client, doc, model) for each pilot doc   # extract_doc must accept a model arg\n     # extract_doc already computes mh_acc (forced per-pair fill-in-blank vs crisp gold)\n     record mean mh_acc, atomic_precision/recall, mean #false_reals/doc, $ spent\n  # PARAMETERIZE extract_doc: replace its hardcoded PRIMARY_MODEL with an\n  # `extractor_model` argument (default 'openai/gpt-4.1-nano' to preserve cache identity).\n  pick STRONG = cheapest candidate with mh_acc >= ACC_THRESHOLD;\n       if none clears 0.45 -> pick the highest-accuracy candidate, record achieved acc,\n       and flag matrix scope = 'extractor strength varied 0.17 -> {achieved}' (see FALLBACK).\n  EMIT phase0 block: {nano_mh_acc, per-candidate mh_acc + cost, chosen STRONG, threshold_cleared}.\n\n############################################################################\n# STAGE 2 -- PER-EXTRACTOR PIPELINE (the only NEW spend; nano is warm-cached)\n############################################################################\n# Generalize SRC/method.run() into run_for_extractor(M): extractor==scorer==decoy-generator=M\n#   (the faithful self-detecting-gate setup; directly tests 'can a competent model\n#    score its OWN errors'). The DENSITY axis holds the scorer fixed within an extractor.\ndef run_for_extractor(M, docs, K=K_SC):\n  EXTRACTION:  reals_by_doc[d] = extract_doc(client, d, rng, extractor_model=M)   # 1 call/doc\n               # crisp 3-way label per real via Doc.label (TRUE/FALSE/UND); record mh_acc\n  DECOYS:      cf_by_doc[d] = gen_counterfactual_decoys(client, d, reals, model=M, rng)  # 1 call/doc\n               # (swap decoys optional negative control; SKIP to save budget unless cheap)\n  SCORING:     for cand in reals + cf_decoys:  zmap[(M,cand_id)] = score_portable(client, M, doc_text, claim)\n               # K=5 isolated provenance-blinded self-consistency; doc-prefix prompt caching ON\n               # (re-uses one cached doc context across the ~K*(#reals+#decoys) calls/doc)\n  RETURN pipe_M = {docs,reals_by_doc,cf_by_doc,all_reals,zmap,ext_meta,...}   # same shape SRC expects\n  # NOTE the only structural change vs SRC: thread `extractor_model`/`scorer_model`=M through\n  #      extract_doc, gen_counterfactual_decoys, score_portable. Everything downstream (norm_pool,\n  #      _pairs_for, diagonal_for_family, analyze_crux) is reused VERBATIM, called with pipe_M.\npipe_nano = run_for_extractor('openai/gpt-4.1-nano', docs)   # ~free via warm cache for 190-prefix\npipe_strong = run_for_extractor(STRONG, docs_strong)         # NEW spend; cost-gate doc count (see STAGE 5)\nsave pipe checkpoints (SRC save_pipe_ckpt pattern) so analysis re-runs need NO API.\n\n############################################################################\n# STAGE 3 -- DENSITY-CONTROLLED SUBSAMPLING (AXIS B; zero API cost)\n############################################################################\ndef subsample_to_density(family_reals, target_false_frac, seed):\n  # family_reals: reals of one family (multi_hop) with crisp label TRUE/FALSE (drop UND).\n  T = [c for c in family_reals if label==TRUE];  F = [c for c in family_reals if label==FALSE]\n  # keep the SMALLER side whole, downsample the larger to hit target fraction; maximize pool size.\n  if target_false_frac high (0.85): keep all F, sample |T| s.t. |F|/(|F|+|T|)==0.85\n  else (0.20/0.50): keep all T, sample |F| s.t. ratio==target\n  rng=Random(seed); shuffle then truncate the downsampled side; PRESERVE doc_id on every kept cand.\n  RETURN set(kept cand_ids)   # the (real, its cf decoy) pairs that ENTER the gate for this cell\n  # Robustness: repeat over SUBSAMPLE_SEEDS=range(10); report median + min/max of realized FDR\n  #             and paired win-rate across seeds so the cell is not a single lucky draw.\n\n############################################################################\n# STAGE 4 -- PER-CELL METRICS  (reuse the iter-3 diagonal + paired block)\n############################################################################\ndef cell_metrics(pipe_M, family, density, seed):\n  norm = norm_pool(pipe_M, SC)                       # per-doc rank-normalized self-consistency Z\n  keep = subsample_to_density(_family_reals(pipe_M,family), density, seed)\n  # Build per_doc pairs restricted to `keep`, exactly like _pairs_for but filtered:\n  per_doc = {doc_id: [ {zr,zd,label,doc_id,w=W_signed_max(zr,zd)} for real in keep with cf decoy scored ]}\n  flat = concat(per_doc.values())\n  rows = []   # the realized-FDR-vs-alpha DIAGONAL\n  for alpha in ALPHA_GRID:\n     T,n_adm_pos,ratio = knockoff_plus_threshold([p.w for p in flat], alpha)  # ratio = decoy_fdr_hat\n     adm = [p for p in flat if p.w>=T];  n_adm=len(adm); n_false=#(adm.label==FALSE)\n     realized = n_false/n_adm\n     ci = doc_block_bootstrap(_doc_arrays(per_doc), stat=_realized_fast(.,alpha), B=B_BOOT, seed=SEED)\n     certified = (n_adm>=k_floor(alpha))\n     populable_at_alpha = (n_false>=... )   # see floor rule below\n     self_report_anti = (realized - ratio) > TAU\n     plain = fc.plain_threshold_gate(raw_self_consistency_Z_of_kept, alpha)  # zero-label foil\n     rows.append({alpha, decoy_fdr_hat=ratio, realized_fdr=realized, ci_low,ci_high,\n                  n_admitted=n_adm, n_false_admitted=n_false, k_floor, certified,\n                  self_report_anti_conservative, plain_realized_fdr})\n  # PAIRED-EXCHANGEABILITY (the KEY readout) -- reuse SRC diagonal_for_family's paired block:\n  Tcut = knockoff_plus_threshold([p.w for p in flat], 0.50)[0];  cut = Tcut if finite else 0.0\n  false_pairs = [p for p in flat if p.label==FALSE]\n  wr_pe,n_tail = tail_win_rate([(p.zr,p.zd) for p in false_pairs], cut)      # decoy wins iff zd>zr\n  ci_pe = doc_block_bootstrap(false_pairs grouped by doc, mean(zd>zr), B=1000, seed=SEED)\n  paired_fails = (ci_pe.ci_high < 0.5)        # false reals systematically beat their OWN decoys\n  paired_ok    = (ci_pe.ci_low <= 0.5 <= ci_pe.ci_high)\n  # MARGINAL crux (decoy ~ spontaneous-error, != true-positive) RESTRICTED to this cell's reals:\n  crux = analyze_crux(pipe_M restricted to family+keep, norm)  # gives decoy_vs_spont ks/mw + decoy_vs_truepos\n  marginal_holds = (crux.tail.decoy_vs_spont.ks_p>0.05 and mw_p>0.05) and (decoy_vs_truepos rejects)\n  RETURN {extractor:M, density, family, mh_acc, n_reals, n_false_total, n_true_total,\n          diagonal_rows:rows, paired:{win_rate:wr_pe, ci:ci_pe, n_tail, paired_fails, paired_ok},\n          marginal:{ks_p,mw_p,verdict,marginal_holds}, seed_spread:{realized,winrate over 10 seeds}}\nCELLS = [ cell_metrics(pipe, fam, rho, seed=SEED) for pipe in {nano,strong} for fam in FAMILIES for rho in DENSITIES ]\n\n# FLOOR / POWER RULE (binding):\n#   A cell is ASSERTED at alpha only if n_admitted>=k_floor(alpha). The DISCONFIRMATION\n#   (anti-conservative) at a given alpha additionally requires n_false_admitted>=N_FALSE_MIN(=40)\n#   OR, if fewer, is reported as 'directional, below false-admission floor'. A clean LOW realized\n#   FDR with CI entirely <= alpha is the POSITIVE 'gate controls' result and does NOT need 40\n#   false admissions (few false admitted IS the good outcome). Cells with NO certified alpha\n#   below 0.5 => 'NO_CERTIFIED_ALPHA' precondition, never 'confirmed by conservatism'.\n\n############################################################################\n# STAGE 5 -- PERSISTENCE MATRIX + EARNED-vs-SCOPED VERDICT (explicit decision rule)\n############################################################################\n# Per cell define (at operative alpha* = most-permissive CERTIFIED alpha, AND also at fixed alpha=0.5):\n#   anti_conservative(c) := realized_fdr > alpha + TAU AND ci_low > alpha          # the primary disconfirmation\n#   gate_controls(c)     := realized_fdr <= alpha + TAU AND NOT(ci_low > alpha)     # ideally ci_high<=alpha at alpha*\n#   paired_fails(c)      := paired.ci_high < 0.5\n#   paired_ok(c)         := paired.ci covers 0.5\n#   marginal_holds(c)    := marginal.marginal_holds\n#   competent(c)         := mh_acc(c.extractor) >= ACC_THRESHOLD\n#   powered(c)           := n_admitted>=k_floor(alpha) (and n_false>=N_FALSE_MIN for a disconfirmation assertion)\n#\n# DECISION RULE (emit verbatim as earned_vs_scoped_verdict.decision_rule):\n#   IF there exist >=2 POWERED competent-extractor cells spanning >=2 densities with\n#      marginal_holds AND (paired_fails OR anti_conservative):\n#         verdict = 'EARNED'  -> 'marginal != paired is a property of the LLM scoring boundary,\n#                                 not an artifact of the weak gpt-4.1-nano extractor; it persists\n#                                 with a competent extractor (mh_acc>=ACC_THRESHOLD) and across\n#                                 false-positive density while the MARGINAL decoy-quality diagnostic\n#                                 is satisfied' => becomes the paper HEADLINE (claim S1c earned).\n#   ELIF the POWERED competent-extractor cells show gate_controls AND paired_ok:\n#         verdict = 'SCOPED'  -> 'the paired failure VANISHES with a competent extractor: the gate\n#                                 controls realized FDR at alpha when the model can score its own\n#                                 errors. Report the POSITIVE result; scope the iter-3 disconfirmation\n#                                 to the weak-scorer / error-dense regime (S1c re-scoped).'\n#   ELIF failure tracks DENSITY (persists at 0.85 for BOTH extractors, vanishes at 0.20 for BOTH):\n#         verdict = 'DENSITY_DRIVEN' -> governing variable is false-positive density, not extractor\n# zero API cost)\\n############################################################################\\ndef subsample_to_density(family_reals, target_false_frac, seed):\\n  # family_reals: reals of one family (multi_hop) with crisp label TRUE/FALSE (drop UND).\\n  T = [c for c in family_reals if label==TRUE];  F = [c for c in family_reals if label==FALSE]\\n  # keep the SMALLER side whole, downsample the larger to hit target fraction; maximize pool size.\\n  if target_false_frac high (0.85): keep all F, sample |T| s.t. |F|/(|F|+|T|)==0.85\\n  else (0.20/0.50): keep all T, sample |F| s.t. ratio==target\\n  rng=Random(seed); shuffle then truncate the downsampled side; PRESERVE doc_id on every kept cand.\\n  RETURN set(kept cand_ids)   # the (real, its cf decoy) pairs that ENTER the gate for this cell\\n  # Robustness: repeat over SUBSAMPLE_SEEDS=range(10); report median + min/max of realized FDR\\n  #             and paired win-rate across seeds so the cell is not a single lucky draw.\\n\\n############################################################################\\n# STAGE 4 -- PER-CELL METRICS  (reuse the iter-3 diagonal + paired block)\\n############################################################################\\ndef cell_metrics(pipe_M, family, density, seed):\\n  norm = norm_pool(pipe_M, SC)                       # per-doc rank-normalized self-consistency Z\\n  keep = subsample_to_density(_family_reals(pipe_M,family), density, seed)\\n  # Build per_doc pairs restricted to `keep`, exactly like _pairs_for but filtered:\\n  per_doc = {doc_id: [ {zr,zd,label,doc_id,w=W_signed_max(zr,zd)} for real in keep with cf decoy scored ]}\\n  flat = concat(per_doc.values())\\n  rows = []   # the realized-FDR-vs-alpha DIAGONAL\\n  for alpha in ALPHA_GRID:\\n     T,n_adm_pos,ratio = knockoff_plus_threshold([p.w for p in flat], alpha)  # ratio = decoy_fdr_hat\\n     adm = [p for p in flat if p.w>=T];  n_adm=len(adm); n_false=#(adm.label==FALSE)\\n     realized = n_false/n_adm\\n     ci = doc_block_bootstrap(_doc_arrays(per_doc), stat=_realized_fast(.,alpha), B=B_BOOT, seed=SEED)\\n     certified = (n_adm>=k_floor(alpha))\\n     populable_at_alpha = (n_false>=... )   # see floor rule below\\n     self_report_anti = (realized - ratio) > TAU\\n     plain = fc.plain_threshold_gate(raw_self_consistency_Z_of_kept, alpha)  # zero-label foil\\n     rows.append({alpha, decoy_fdr_hat=ratio, realized_fdr=realized, ci_low,ci_high,\\n                  n_admitted=n_adm, n_false_admitted=n_false, k_floor, certified,\\n                  self_report_anti_conservative, plain_realized_fdr})\\n  # PAIRED-EXCHANGEABILITY (the KEY readout) -- reuse SRC diagonal_for_family's paired block:\\n  Tcut = knockoff_plus_threshold([p.w for p in flat], 0.50)[0];  cut = Tcut if finite else 0.0\\n  false_pairs = [p for p in flat if p.label==FALSE]\\n  wr_pe,n_tail = tail_win_rate([(p.zr,p.zd) for p in false_pairs], cut)      # decoy wins iff zd>zr\\n  ci_pe = doc_block_bootstrap(false_pairs grouped by doc, mean(zd>zr), B=1000, seed=SEED)\\n  paired_fails = (ci_pe.ci_high < 0.5)        # false reals systematically beat their OWN decoys\\n  paired_ok    = (ci_pe.ci_low <= 0.5 <= ci_pe.ci_high)\\n  # MARGINAL crux (decoy ~ spontaneous-error, != true-positive) RESTRICTED to this cell's reals:\\n  crux = analyze_crux(pipe_M restricted to family+keep, norm)  # gives decoy_vs_spont ks/mw + decoy_vs_truepos\\n  marginal_holds = (crux.tail.decoy_vs_spont.ks_p>0.05 and mw_p>0.05) and (decoy_vs_truepos rejects)\\n  RETURN {extractor:M, density, family, mh_acc, n_reals, n_false_total, n_true_total,\\n          diagonal_rows:rows, paired:{win_rate:wr_pe, ci:ci_pe, n_tail, paired_fails, paired_ok},\\n          marginal:{ks_p,mw_p,verdict,marginal_holds}, seed_spread:{realized,winrate over 10 seeds}}\\nCELLS = [ cell_metrics(pipe, fam, rho, seed=SEED) for pipe in {nano,strong} for fam in FAMILIES for rho in DENSITIES ]\\n\\n# FLOOR / POWER RULE (binding):\\n#   A cell is ASSERTED at alpha only if n_admitted>=k_floor(alpha). The DISCONFIRMATION\\n#   (anti-conservative) at a given alpha additionally requires n_false_admitted>=N_FALSE_MIN(=40)\\n#   OR, if fewer, is reported as 'directional, below false-admission floor'. A clean LOW realized\\n#   FDR with CI entirely <= alpha is the POSITIVE 'gate controls' result and does NOT need 40\\n#   false admissions (few false admitted IS the good outcome). Cells with NO certified alpha\\n#   below 0.5 => 'NO_CERTIFIED_ALPHA' precondition, never 'confirmed by conservatism'.\\n\\n############################################################################\\n# STAGE 5 -- PERSISTENCE MATRIX + EARNED-vs-SCOPED VERDICT (explicit decision rule)\\n############################################################################\\n# Per cell define (at operative alpha* = most-permissive CERTIFIED alpha, AND also at fixed alpha=0.5):\\n#   anti_conservative(c) := realized_fdr > alpha + TAU AND ci_low > alpha          # the primary disconfirmation\\n#   gate_controls(c)     := realized_fdr <= alpha + TAU AND NOT(ci_low > alpha)     # ideally ci_high<=alpha at alpha*\\n#   paired_fails(c)      := paired.ci_high < 0.5\\n#   paired_ok(c)         := paired.ci covers 0.5\\n#   marginal_holds(c)    := marginal.marginal_holds\\n#   competent(c)         := mh_acc(c.extractor) >= ACC_THRESHOLD\\n#   powered(c)           := n_admitted>=k_floor(alpha) (and n_false>=N_FALSE_MIN for a disconfirmation assertion)\\n#\\n# DECISION RULE (emit verbatim as earned_vs_scoped_verdict.decision_rule):\\n#   IF there exist >=2 POWERED competent-extractor cells spanning >=2 densities with\\n#      marginal_holds AND (paired_fails OR anti_conservative):\\n#         verdict = 'EARNED'  -> 'marginal != paired is a property of the LLM scoring boundary,\\n#                                 not an artifact of the weak gpt-4.1-nano extractor; it persists\\n#                                 with a competent extractor (mh_acc>=ACC_THRESHOLD) and across\\n#                                 false-positive density while the MARGINAL decoy-quality diagnostic\\n#                                 is satisfied' => becomes the paper HEADLINE (claim S1c earned).\\n#   ELIF the POWERED competent-extractor cells show gate_controls AND paired_ok:\\n#         verdict = 'SCOPED'  -> 'the paired failure VANISHES with a competent extractor: the gate\\n#                                 controls realized FDR at alpha when the model can score its own\\n#                                 errors. Report the POSITIVE result; scope the iter-3 disconfirmation\\n#                                 to the weak-scorer / error-dense regime (S1c re-scoped).'\\n#   ELIF failure tracks DENSITY (persists at 0.85 for BOTH extractors, vanishes at 0.20 for BOTH):\\n#         verdict = 'DENSITY_DRIVEN' -> governing variable is false-positive density, not extractor\\n#                                 competence; report the density crossover explicitly.\\n#   ELSE: verdict = 'UNDERPOWERED_INCONCLUSIVE' -> not enough powered cells to separate hypotheses\\n#                                 (the failure the floor/power rule is designed to prevent); list\\n#                                 which cells fell below k_floor / N_FALSE_MIN.\\n# matrix = 2 (extractor) x 3 (density) x 2 (family) table of {realized_fdr(+CI), decoy_fdr_hat,\\n#          paired win-rate(+CI), marginal verdict, anti_conservative/gate_controls flags, powered}.\\n# BH (st.benjamini_hochberg, q=0.05) across ALL cell p-values (marginal ks/mw + paired ks per cell).\\n# SANITY ANCHOR: the nano x 0.85 x multi_hop cell MUST reproduce the iter-3 headline\\n#   (realized FDR ~1.0 at alpha*=0.5, paired win-rate <0.5) -- assert + log; if not, STOP and debug\\n#   (warm-cache mismatch) before spending on the strong extractor.\\n\\n############################################################################\\n# STAGE 6 -- FIGURES (full captions) + OUTPUT (exp_gen_sol_out schema)\\n############################################################################\\n# Figures (Agg backend, .jpg into figures/), each caption carrying the 1/k floor, doc-block\\n# bootstrap CIs, and the persist/vanish reading:\\n#  F1 persistence heatmap: anti_conservative flag / realized FDR across (extractor x density) at alpha*,\\n#     cells annotated with n_admitted, n_false, decoy_fdr_hat, 'below floor' hatching.\\n#  F2 realized-FDR-vs-alpha diagonals: nano vs strong overlaid at matched density (0.85 and 0.50),\\n#     ideal y=x dashed, 1/k floor shaded, doc-block CIs as error bars, plain-baseline + (optional) swap dotted.\\n#  F3 paired win-rate over FALSE pairs (+CI) per cell with the 0.5 exchangeable line -- THE persist/vanish chart;\\n#     annotate the paired-win asymmetry (mean(zd>zr)).\\n#  F4 marginal crux CDF overlay (true-positive / spontaneous-error / counterfactual-decoy) per extractor,\\n#     to show MARGINAL holds while PAIRED differs across extractors.\\n# OUTPUT method_out.json via SRC build_output pattern, schema 'exp_gen_sol_out':\\n#   {metadata:{...}, datasets:[{dataset:'CLUTRR-v1-CrispGold-CalibrationAnchor', examples:[...]}]}\\n#   metadata MUST include: phase0_extractor_probe, persistence_matrix (full 2x3x2),\\n#     per-cell {diagonal_rows incl (alpha,decoy_fdr_hat,realized,ci) TRIPLE, paired, marginal},\\n#     earned_vs_scoped_verdict{verdict, decision_rule(verbatim), supporting_cells},\\n#     extraction_quality per extractor (mh_acc, atomic P/R), dataset_counts, hyperparameters,\\n#     bh_correction, figure-ready arrays, full_figure_captions{F1..F4}, runtime+cost_trace_path.\\n#   examples[]: one per scored real carrying input(JSON: doc_id,head,relation,tail,claim,extractor),\\n#     output=crisp label, metadata_* (z_real, z_decoy, w, fact_type, density_membership flags,\\n#     per-alpha admit predictions). VALIDATE with the aii-json skill against exp_gen_sol_out.\\n#   If method_out.json > file-size limit, use aii-file-size-limit skill to split + emit mini/preview.\\n# Run order (gradual scaling, cost-gated): --selftest -> --mini(3 docs both extractors) ->\\n#   phase0 probe -> nano full (warm) -> strong --n-docs 40 checkpoint (CHECK cost+populability) ->\\n#   strong full (cap doc count so projected $ <= soft cap $4). Log cost after EVERY call (cost.jsonl).\\n#   Background+PID launch (uv run method.py & PID=$!), never block-poll a long foreground run.\",\n  \"fallback_plan\": \"EXTRACTOR (Axis A) cannot clear 0.45: (a) lower the bar to the best achievable and report the matrix as 'extractor strength varied 0.17 -> {achieved_mh_acc}'; even a jump to ~0.30-0.40 meaningfully de-confounds. (b) If NO candidate beats ~0.20 on multi_hop (CLUTRR long-chain kinship is genuinely hard), pivot the de-confound onto a LESS error-dense FAMILY: run the diagonal on ATOMIC facts (directly stated, low intrinsic error) with gpt-4.1-nano -- atomic is the natural 'competent' regime for the same model, giving a within-model strength contrast at zero extra-model cost. (c) Try one strong open model via OpenRouter (e.g. a Qwen/Llama-70B-class instruct) if OpenAI minis underperform; pick on Phase-0 mh_acc/$.\\nBUDGET overrun on the strong extractor: cut strong-extractor docs first (120 -> 80 -> 40), then drop the swap negative control and entrapment/ladder/verbalized entirely (NOT needed for dir2's core), then reduce K self-consistency 5->3 for the strong arm only (record K per cell in metadata; note the small reduction in score resolution), then restrict to multi_hop only. The nano arm is warm-cached and ~free regardless. Hard stop at $10 is enforced by llm_client BudgetExceeded; on hard stop, emit whatever cells completed with the matrix flagged partial.\\nFLOOR not reached (strong extractor yields too few FALSE reals for 0.85 density or <40 false admissions): (a) lean on Axis B subsampling -- 0.50/0.20 cells still populate; (b) scale strong-extractor docs up (more k>=6 long chains => more multi_hop errors) within budget; (c) report the under-floor cell as a PRECONDITION ('directional, below false-admission floor'), never as a conclusion. A clean low realized FDR with CI<=alpha is still the valid POSITIVE 'gate controls' result and needs only n_admitted>=k_floor, not 40 false.\\nNO certified alpha below 0.5 in a cell: report 'NO_CERTIFIED_ALPHA' (a precondition outcome) for that cell; the matrix verdict then rests on the cells that ARE certified.\\nHIGH subsample variance: the 10-seed robustness loop already reports spread; if a cell's realized FDR / win-rate flips sign across seeds, mark it UNSTABLE and exclude from the EARNED/SCOPED count (treat as underpowered).\\nWARM-CACHE / sanity-anchor mismatch: if the nano x 0.85 x multi_hop cell does NOT reproduce the iter-3 headline (realized ~1.0 at alpha*=0.5, paired win-rate <0.5), STOP before spending on the strong extractor -- the bug is in corpus regeneration (doc-prefix ordering) or model/prompt drift, not the science; diff the regenerated 190-prefix doc_ids against iter-3 and fix before proceeding.\\nWORST CASE (API/quota dies early): the nano warm-cached cells + Phase-0 probe alone still deliver a partial matrix and an honest 'INCONCLUSIVE/underpowered, only the weak-extractor point reproduced' verdict -- which is a faithful, publishable scoping statement, not a vacuous null.\\nOPTIONAL EXTENSION if budget remains under $4: add ONE cross-scorer cell (strong extractor's facts scored by gpt-4.1-nano, G!=S) and compute the PAIRED win-rate there too, partially satisfying the hypothesis's 'compute the paired statistic across (G,S) configs' (S2b); if not run, state plainly in metadata that paired de-circularization remains marginal-only.\",\n  \"testing_plan\": \"1) OFFLINE FIRST (no API, no cost): `uv run method.py --selftest`. Keep every existing iter-3 assert (knockoff+ vs vectorized _knockoff_fast equality over 200 random arrays, W signed-max antisymmetry, fair-coin win-rate in (0.45,0.55), too-easy decoy win-rate<0.45 + KS sig, doc-block CI > iid CI, Doc.label crisp 3-way, BH monotonic, entrapment estimators, rank_normalize). Must be green before any network call.\\n2) MINI SMOKE (~cents): `uv run method.py --mini` (3 docs) for BOTH extractors -- confirm extraction JSON parses, gen_counterfactual_decoys returns non-empty, score_portable returns floats in [0,1], cost logs to cost.jsonl, cache files written. No crashes through cell_metrics on the tiny pool.\\n3) PHASE-0 PROBE (~$0.1-0.3): run the extractor probe on ~40 pilot docs; PRINT mh_acc + atomic P/R + $/doc per candidate. CONFIRMATION SIGNAL: at least one candidate's multi-hop accuracy is clearly > 0.17 (ideally >= 0.45) and gpt-4.1-nano reproduces ~0.169. Pick the cheapest clearing the bar; abort-to-fallback if none.\\n4) NANO SANITY ANCHOR (~free, warm cache): run the nano arm + cell_metrics on multi_hop x 0.85 (native density). CONFIRMATION SIGNAL: realized FDR ~1.0 at alpha*=0.5 with CI [~0.66,1.0], paired win-rate <0.5 -- i.e. the iter-3 headline reproduces. If it does not, STOP and debug warm-cache/corpus ordering (see fallback) -- do NOT spend on the strong extractor until this matches.\\n5) STRONG-EXTRACTOR CHECKPOINT (`--n-docs 40`): run the strong arm on 40 docs; inspect populability (n_false reals per family per density) and the cost trajectory. CONFIRMATION SIGNAL: projected full-run cost (linear extrapolation) <= soft cap $4 AND at least the 0.50/0.85 multi_hop cells reach n_admitted>=k_floor(0.5)=2 (and ideally toward N_FALSE_MIN at full scale). name: project_deconfound_iter4_plan
description: run_MQN7mBg4AhvH iter4 GEN_PLAN experiment_2 (dir2 P1-DECONFOUND) — 2-axis extractor×density persistence-matrix plan for marginal-vs-paired knockoff+ failure

GEN_PLAN for run_MQN7mBg4AhvH invention-loop iter_4, artifact experiment_iter4_dir2 (P1-DECONFOUND). Plan written to gen_plan_experiment_2/.terminal_claude_agent_struct_out.json. Resolves reviewer methodology-MAJOR: de-confound the iter-3 disconfirmation (realized FDR 1.0 at alpha*=0.5, paired sign-flip fail on 12 multi_hop pairs) from a pathological extractor (gpt-4.1-nano forced multi-hop acc 0.169, ~85% genuine-false). Builds on [[project_invloop_iter3_plan]] + [[project_decoyfdr_iter2_results]] ([[project_knockoff_gated_neurosymbolic]] hypothesis).

**Plan essence — controlled factorial, persist/vanish matrix:**
- AXIS A extractor strength: gpt-4.1-nano (baseline) vs >=1 Phase-0-probed stronger model (mh_acc >> 0.17, ideally >=0.45), used as extractor==scorer==decoy-generator (model scores its OWN errors — the faithful self-detecting-gate test).
- AXIS B false-positive density: post-hoc stratified subsampling of the SCORED real pool to ~20/50/85% genuine-false — FREE (reuses cached scores, scorer fixed), decoupled from extractor strength.
- Per (extractor×density×family) cell: realized-FDR-vs-alpha diagonal + doc-block bootstrap B>=2000 CIs + decoy_fdr_hat + PAIRED win-rate over FALSE pairs at cutoff (key readout) + MARGINAL crux (decoy~spontaneous != true-pos).
- EARNED-vs-SCOPED decision rule stated verbatim in output: paired failure PERSISTS in >=2 powered competent cells w/ marginal holding => EARNED headline 'marginal!=paired at LLM boundary'; VANISHES (gate controls FDR) => SCOPED to weak/error-dense regime + positive result; DENSITY_DRIVEN / UNDERPOWERED sub-verdicts.

**NON-OBVIOUS reuse map (art_sBLQqsdm3EIA = iter_3/gen_art/gen_art_experiment_1, the runnable P1 self-consistency diagonal — NOT iter3 exp3=P3 regime-diag):**
- COPY method.py + fdr_stats.py + fdr_core.py + llm_client.py + data.py + cache/ into the workspace and EXTEND; don't reimplement the gate.
- The only structural change: parameterize `extract_doc`, `gen_counterfactual_decoys(model=)`, `score_portable(model=)` by extractor_model (currently hardcode PRIMARY_MODEL='openai/gpt-4.1-nano'). Everything downstream reused verbatim: `diagonal_for_family` (already returns decoy_fdr_hat=knockoff+ ratio + a `paired_exchangeability` block w/ tail_win_rate_false_pairs), `_pairs_for`, `norm_pool`, `analyze_crux`, `st.knockoff_plus_threshold`/`_knockoff_fast`/`tail_win_rate`/`doc_block_bootstrap`/`rank_normalize`/`k_floor`/`benjamini_hochberg`, `fc.plain_threshold_gate`.
- llm_client `OpenRouterClient.call(model, messages, max_tokens, temperature, seed, sample_idx)` — model is already a per-call arg; disk cache keyed sha256(payload+sample_idx); exact usage.cost; fallback_cache_dirs warm-start; BudgetExceeded hard-stop. nano 190-doc prefix is warm-cached (iter2 exp2 + iter3 exp1 cache/) => nano arm ~free; only the strong extractor is new spend.
- ALPHA_GRID [.05,.1,.2,.3,.5], k_floor {20,10,5,4,2}; SEED=20240617; PYTHONHASHSEED=0; output schema `exp_gen_sol_out` {metadata, datasets:[{dataset,examples}]}; subsample preserves doc_id so doc-block bootstrap intact.

**Cost:** nano ~free; strong extractor (gpt-4.1-mini ~$0.40/$1.60) ~$0.016/doc w/ K=5 SC scoring of reals+cf decoys => ~120-160 docs ≈ $3. Soft cap $4 / hard $10. Gradual scale: --selftest -> --mini -> phase0 probe -> nano sanity-anchor (must reproduce iter-3 realized~1.0/winrate<0.5 before spending on strong) -> strong --n-docs 40 checkpoint -> full. Background+PID, never block-poll.

Sibling iter4 plans: [[project_appanchor_iter4_plan]] [[project_problog_iter4_plan]]. Related: [[project_p3_regime_diagnostic]] [[project_clutrr_crispgold_anchor]].

### [49] ASSISTANT · 2026-06-16 10:50:50 UTC

```
Plan complete and written to `.terminal_claude_agent_struct_out.json`.

## What the plan delivers

The artifact direction's single ask — **de-confound the iteration-3 disconfirmation from a pathological extractor** — is operationalized as a controlled 2-axis factorial, built by *reusing the exact iter-3 P1 code* (`art_sBLQqsdm3EIA` = `iter_3/gen_art/gen_art_experiment_1`) rather than rebuilding the gate:

- **Axis A — extractor strength:** gpt-4.1-nano (baseline, mh-acc 0.169) vs a Phase-0-probed stronger model (target ≥0.45), each run as **extractor == scorer == decoy-generator** so the model scores its *own* errors — the faithful test of "can a competent model avoid the paired failure."
- **Axis B — false-positive density:** stratified post-hoc subsampling of the *already-scored* pool to ~20/50/85% genuine-false. This is **free** (no new API) and holds the scorer fixed, cleanly decoupling density from extractor competence.
- **Per cell:** realized-FDR-vs-α diagonal + doc-block bootstrap (B≥2000) CIs + `decoy_fdr_hat` + the **paired win-rate over FALSE pairs** (the key readout) + the **marginal crux** — so "marginal holds while paired fails" is testable cell-by-cell.
- **Verdict:** an explicit **EARNED-vs-SCOPED decision rule** emitted verbatim in `method_out.json`, with `N_false_min=40`/`k_floor` power gating, BH correction, a nano sanity-anchor that must reproduce the iter-3 headline before spending on the strong arm, and full figure captions.

## Key design decisions surfaced
- The **only structural code change** is threading `extractor_model` through `extract_doc` / `gen_counterfactual_decoys` / `score_portable`; the entire diagonal + paired-exchangeability + crux machinery is reused verbatim.
- **Cost** stays under the ~$4 soft cap: the nano arm is warm-cached (≈free); only the strong extractor (~$0.016/doc at K=5) drives spend (~$3 for ~120–160 docs), gated by gradual scaling.
- Fallbacks cover the realistic risk that **no model clears 0.45 on CLUTRR multi-hop** (pivot to atomic-family or an open model; even 0.30–0.40 de-confounds), budget overrun, and under-floor cells (reported as preconditions, never "confirmed by conservatism").

Compute profile: `cpu_heavy` (CPU-only, async I/O bound, vectorized bootstrap). Memory index updated.
```
